<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Item&nbsp;1.01 Entry into Material Definitive Agreement.</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;LOAN AGREEMENT WITH NATEXIS BANQUES POPULAIRES


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;On December&nbsp;23, 2004, subject to obtaining approval of the French
government, Toreador Resources Corporation, a Delaware corporation (the
&#147;<B><I>Company</I></B>&#148;) as an Obligor, and its subsidiaries Madison Energy France, a <I>soci&#233;t&#233;
en commandite simple </I>incorporated under the laws of France (&#147;<B><I>MEF</I></B>&#148;) as the
Borrower, Madison Oil France, a <I>soci&#233;t&#233; anonyme </I>incorporcated under the laws of
France (&#147;<B><I>MOF</I></B>&#148;) as a Guarantor, and Madison Oil Company Europe, a Delaware
Corporation (&#147;<B><I>MOCE</I></B>&#148;) as an Obligor entered into a Reserve Base Revolving
Facility Agreement (the &#147;<B><I>Revolving Facility Agreement</I></B>&#148;) with Natexis Banques
Populaires, a French bank (the &#147;<B><I>Agent</I></B>&#148;) and certain lenders party thereto (the
&#147;<B><I>Lenders</I></B>&#148;). While there can be no assurances that approval of the French
government will be obtained, it is anticipated that such approval will be
obtained within 60&nbsp;days after December&nbsp;23, 2004. The Revolving Facility
Agreement provides that upon certain specified conditions being met, the
Lenders shall make borrowing base loans to MEF during the period from December
23, 2004 through December&nbsp;23, 2009 up to an aggregate amount of fifteen million
dollars (US$15,000,000). The proceeds of the loans will be used for general
corporate purposes, to develop certain hydrocarbon fields currently owned by
MEF, and to finance the acquisition and development of additional hydrocarbon
fields in France and Turkey.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The loans will be secured by assignments of certain contract rights,
including our rights in the French fields, pledges of ownership interests of
MOF and MEF, and collateralization of a collection account of MEF. The
interest rate on the loans will be the LIBOR rate plus 2.25-2.75%, depending on
the amount of principal outstanding. Principal payments, together with accrued
interest, will be due in monthly installments. MOF, MOCE and Toreador will
each enter into unconditional guarantees of MEF&#146;s obligations.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Revolving Facility Agreement contains affirmative and negative
covenants with which the parties to the Revolving Facility Agreement, including
the Company, must comply, including reporting requirements, restrictions on
indebtedness, restrictions on granting liens, meeting certain ratios, and
restrictions on paying dividends on its capital stock. The events of default
under the Revolving Facility Agreement include payment defaults, breaches of
covenants, cross defaults with certain other indebtedness, and insolvency
events.


<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Item&nbsp;2.03 Creation of a Direct Financial Obligation or an Obligation Under an
Off-Balance Sheet Arrangement of a Registrant.</B>



<P align="left" style="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;See Item&nbsp;1.01 &#150; Entry into Material Definitive Agreement, discussing the
Revolving Facility Agreement by and among the Company, MEF, MOF, MOCE, Agent
and Lenders.

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>SECTION 1<BR>
INTERPRETATION</B>



<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">In this Agreement:


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Activity Report</B>&#148; means the activity report to be prepared monthly by the
Borrower, to be delivered to the Agent in accordance with paragraph
19.3.1, similar to the form of the Activity Report delivered to the Agent
for July&nbsp;2004 but as may be modified from time to time by the Borrower
and/or TRC (in which case it shall be in form and substance satisfactory
to the Agent acting reasonably).


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Additional Cost Rate</B>&#148; has the meaning given to it in Schedule&nbsp;5 (<I>Mandatory Cost </I>Formulae).


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Affiliate</B>&#148; means, in relation to any person, a Subsidiary of that person
or a Holding Company of that person or any other Subsidiary of that
Holding Company.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Asset Life Cover Ratio</B>&#148; or &#147;<B>ALCR</B>&#148; means, on any Ratio Calculation Date,
the ratio of:


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the NPV (9)&nbsp;for the period from the relevant Ratio Calculation
Date to the Reserves Tail Date plus an amount equal to any monies
standing to the credit of the Collection Account at 11.00 am (Paris
time) as at such date; to</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the Outstanding Amount (after any repayment of the Facility
made on such Ratio Calculation Date).</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Assigned Rights</B>&#148; means the rights of the Borrower to receive payments
under the Sale and Purchase Contracts, the Insurance Policy and the Hedge
Agreements, as assigned to the Agent (acting on behalf of the Lenders)
pursuant to the Assignment Agreements.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Assignment Agreements</B>&#148; means the Insurance Policy Delegation Agreement
and Master Receivables Assignment Agreement.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Authorisation</B>&#148; means an authorisation, consent, approval, resolution,
licence, exemption, filing, notarisation or registration.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Availability Period</B>&#148; means the period from the date on which the Lenders
are satisfied that the conditions precedent listed in Schedule&nbsp;2
(<I>Conditions precedent</I>) have been met to the date which is thirty days
before the Final Maturity Date.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Available Amount</B>&#148; means (a)&nbsp;the Maximum Amount minus (b)&nbsp;the Outstanding
Amount.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Borrowing Base</B>&#148; has the meaning ascribed to that term in Clause 6.2
(<I>Borrowing Base Determination</I>)


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">- 2 -
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">




<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Borrowing Base Deficiency</B>&#148; means the amount by which the aggregate of the
Outstanding Amount and all accrued but unpaid fees and interest under the
Finance Documents exceeds the then applicable Maximum Amount.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Borrowing Base Determination Date</B>&#148; means (i)&nbsp;Closing Date, 30 June&nbsp;2005,
30 December&nbsp;2005, 30 June&nbsp;2006, 30 December&nbsp;2006, 30 June&nbsp;2007, 30
December&nbsp;2007, 30 June&nbsp;2008, 30 December&nbsp;2008 and 30 June&nbsp;2009, (ii)&nbsp;any
other date on which the Borrowing Base is re-set at the request of the
Agent in accordance with paragraph 6.2.8 and (iii)&nbsp;any other date on which
the Borrowing Base is re-set at the request of the Borrower in accordance
with paragraph 6.2.9.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Borrowing Base Reduction Schedule</B>&#148; means the schedule of reduction of the
Borrowing Base as determined in accordance with Clause 6.2 (<I>Borrowing Base
Determination</I>).


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Borrowing Base Utilisation Ratio</B>&#148; means, on any date, the ratio of (a)
the aggregate of (i)&nbsp;the Outstanding Amount as at such date and (ii)&nbsp;all
fees and interest payable under the Finance Documents as at such date to
(b)&nbsp;the Maximum Amount as at such date, such ratio being expressed as a
percentage.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Break Costs</B>&#148; means the amount (if any) by which:


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the interest which a Lender should have received for the period
from the date of receipt of all or any part of its participation in a
Loan or Unpaid Sum to the last day of the current Interest Period in
respect of that Loan or Unpaid Sum, had the principal amount or
Unpaid Sum received been paid on the last day of that Interest
Period;</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">exceeds:


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the amount which that Lender would be able to obtain by placing
an amount equal to the principal amount or Unpaid Sum received by it
on deposit with a leading bank in the Relevant Interbank Market for a
period starting on the Business Day following receipt or recovery and
ending on the last day of the current Interest Period.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Business Day</B>&#148; means a day (other than a Saturday or Sunday) on which
banks are open for general business in London, New York and Paris.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>CEP</B>&#148; means Cifal Elan Petroleum Services Ltd, represented by Cifal,
acting as engineer advisor to the Technical Bank.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>CEP Report</B>&#148; means the report delivered by CEP in the month of September
2003.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Code</B>&#148; means, at any date, the U.S. Internal Revenue Code of 1986 and the
regulations promulgated and the judicial and administrative decisions
rendered under it, all as the same may be in effect at such date.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Collection Account</B>&#148; means the account opened in the name of the Borrower
in the books of the Agent (and any renewal or any redesignation thereof),
on which all monies relating to the Assigned Rights are to be paid, and
pledged in favour of the Lenders pursuant to the Pledge over Account
Agreement.

<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Consolidated Indebtedness</B>&#148; means on a consolidated basis, at any time

constituting Financial Indebtedness excluding (i)&nbsp;any Financial
Indebtedness of any Group member to another Group member and (ii)
indebtedness whose contractual maturity exceeds by more than one year the
Final Maturity Date and qualifying as equity (<I>fonds propres</I>) or

immediately above the debt owed to the shareholders but below any
non-secured indebtedness of the Group.

United States, as the case may be.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Grace Period</B>&#148; means the period from and including the date of execution
of this Agreement to and including the date falling six (6)&nbsp;months after
the date of execution of this Agreement.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Group</B>&#148; means TRC, MOCE, MOF, the Borrower and any of their Subsidiaries.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Guarantee</B>&#148; means the guarantee (<I>caution solidaire</I>) granted by the
Guarantor pursuant to Clause 22 (<I>Guarantee</I>) of this Agreement.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Guaranteed Obligations</B>&#148; has the meaning given to it in Clause 22
(<I>Guarantee</I>) of this Agreement.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Hedge Agreements</B>&#148; means the interest, currency or commodity swap, option,
cap, collar, floor or similar arrangement or other hedge arrangements
entered into by the Borrower with the Hedge Providers in terms
satisfactory to the Agent in accordance with Clause 21.22 (<I>Hedge
Agreements</I>), and maintained as long as all obligations under the Finance
Documents have not been fully discharged, in terms sufficient to cover all
payment obligations of the Borrower under the Facility.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Hedge Providers</B>&#148; means the financial institutions, international trading
institutions and/or the Purchaser, reasonably agreed in writing in advance
by the Agent, which shall enter into the Hedge Agreements with the
Borrower.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Holding Company</B>&#148; means, in relation to a company or corporation, any
other company or corporation in respect of which it is a Subsidiary.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Indebtedness Ratio</B>&#148; means, on any Ratio Calculation Date, the ratio of
(a)&nbsp;Consolidated Stockholder Equity to (b)&nbsp;Consolidated Indebtedness
(excluding Consolidated Stockholder Equity).


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Independent Engineering Consultant</B>&#148; means CEP or any other independent

and the Borrower.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Insurance Policy</B>&#148; means the insurance policy subscribed by the Borrower
to cover all damages and liabilities likely to be incurred in connection
with its activities (Energy Package) with AGF effective on 1 April&nbsp;2003,
and/or any other insurance policy satisfactory to the Agent covering
damages and liabilities in connection with the activities of the Borrower
(and its Subsidiaries) in hydrocarbons in relation to the Fields.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Insurance Policy Delegation Agreement</B>&#148; means the delegation agreement

<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>NPV (9)</B>&#148; means the net present value, as at the date of calculation, of

<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Outstanding Amount</B>&#148; means the aggregate principal amount of the Loans
which have been made available to the Borrower under the Facility and
which remain outstanding at any considered time.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Party</B>&#148; means a party to this Agreement.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>PBGC</B>&#148; means the U.S. Pension Benefit Guaranty Corporation, or any entity
succeeding to all or any of its functions under ERISA.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Permitted Encumbrance</B>&#148; means the Encumbrances permitted in accordance
with Clause 21.7 (<I>Negative pledge</I>).


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Permitted Financial Indebtedness</B>&#148; means (i)&nbsp;any loan made within the
Group by a member of the Group to another member of the Group not
exceeding in aggregate USD 500,000 and (ii)&nbsp;any loans (other than loans
made pursuant to sub-paragraph (i)) made within the Group by a member of
the Group to another member of the Group for the purpose of financing the
development of hydrocarbon fields in Turkey.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Petroleum</B>&#148; means any mineral oil or relative hydrocarbon and natural gas
existing in its natural condition in strata but not including coal or
bituminous shales or other stratified deposits from which oil can be
extracted by destructive distillation.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Pledge over Account Agreement</B>&#148; means the agreement entered into at latest
on the first Utilisation Date between the Borrower and the Finance Parties
pursuant to which the Borrower has granted a pledge over the Collection
Account in favour of the Finance Parties.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Pre Debt Cashflows</B>&#148; means the net cashflows derived from the exploitation
of the Proved Reserves. In calculating these cashflows, capital
expenditures, general and administrative costs, operative costs in
relation with the Fields exploitation, payments to other debt providers
and creditors, proceeds or outgoings from the Hedge Agreements, income
taxes and other taxes and withholdings will be taken into account.
However, interest, fees and repayments under the Facility will not be
included, although the effect of those payments on taxes and withholdings
will be included. At the discretion of the Technical Bank and for the
account of the Borrower, capital and operating costs shall be verified by
the Independent Engineering Consultant.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Proved Reserves</B>&#148; means, at the time of an estimate, such quantities of
Petroleum deriving from the Fields which by analysis of geological and
engineering data, can be estimated with reasonable certainty to be
commercially recoverable, from a given date forward, from known reservoirs
and under current economic conditions, operating methods, and government
regulations. Establishment of current economic conditions should include
relevant historical Petroleum prices and associated costs and may involve
an averaging period that is consistent with the purpose of the reserves
estimate, appropriate contract obligations, corporate procedures, and
government regulations involved in reporting these reserves. In general,
reserves are considered proved if the commercial productibility of the
reservoir is supported by actual production or formation tests. In this
context, the term &#147;proved&#148; refers to the actual quantities of Petroleum
reserves and not just the productivity of the well or reservoir. In
certain cases, Proved Reserves may be assigned on the basis of well logs
and/or core analysis that indicate the subject reservoir is hydrocarbon
bearing and is analogous to reservoirs in the same area that are producing
or have demonstrated the ability to produce on formation tests. The area


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">- 13 -
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">




<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">of the reservoir considered as &#147;proved&#148; includes (1)&nbsp;the area delineated
by drilling and defined by fluid contacts, if any, and (2)&nbsp;the undrilled
portions of the reservoir that can reasonably be judged as commercially
productive on the basis of available geological and engineering data. In
the absence of data on fluid contacts, the lowest known occurrence of
hydrocarbons controls the proved limit unless otherwise indicated by
definitive geological, engineering or performance data. Reserves may be
classified as &#147;proved&#148; in accordance with the principles approved by the
board of directors of the Society of Petroleum Engineers, Inc. and the
executive board of the World Petroleum Congress in March&nbsp;1997, if
facilities to process and transport those reserves to market are
operational at the time of the estimate or there is a reasonable
expectation that such facilities will be installed. Reserves which are to
be produced through the application of established improved recovery
methods are included in the proved classification when (1)&nbsp;successful
testing by a pilot project or favorable response of an installed program
in the same or an analogous reservoir with similar rock and fluid
properties provides support for the analysis on which the project was
based, and (2)&nbsp;it is reasonably certain that the project will proceed.
Reserves to be recovered by improved recovery methods that have yet to be
established through commercially successful applications are included in
the proved classification only (1)&nbsp;after a favorable production response
from the subject reservoir from either (a)&nbsp;a representative pilot or (b)
an installed program where the response provides support for the analysis
on which the project is based and (2)&nbsp;it is reasonably certain the project
will proceed.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Proved Developed Producing Reserves (PDP Reserves)</B>&#148; means the fraction of
the Proved Reserves expected to be recovered from completion intervals
which are open and producing at the time of the estimate. Improved
recovery reserves are considered producing only after the improved
recovery project is in operation.


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">&#147;<B>Purchaser</B>&#148; means Total and/or any other reputable oil trading company
which has been agreed in writing by the Agent in advance (which agreement
by the Agent shall not be unreasonably withheld or delayed by the Agent)
or which is paying though letters of credit issued by banks that have been
agreed in writing by the Agent in advance (which agreement by the Agent

    <TD>a &#147;<B>security interest</B>&#148; includes any type of
security (<I>s&#251;ret&#233; r&#233;elle</I>) and transfer by way of security;</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>&#147;<B>wilful misconduct</B>&#148; means &#147;<I>dol</I>&#148;;</TD>

    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(m)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>a provision of law is a reference to that
provision as amended or re-enacted; and</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>unless a contrary indication appears, a time of
day is a reference to Paris time.</TD>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>SECTION 2<BR>
THE FACILITY</B>



<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">2.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>THE FACILITY</B></TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">2.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Facility</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">Subject to the terms of this Agreement, the Lenders make available to the
Borrower a reserve base revolving loan facility for an aggregate amount
equal to the Total Commitments.


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">2.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Finance Parties&#146; rights and obligations</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">2.2.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The obligations of each Finance Party under the Finance
Documents are several (<I>conjointes et non solidaires</I>). Failure by a
Finance Party to perform its obligations under the Finance Documents
does not affect the obligations of any other Party under the Finance
Documents. No Finance Party is responsible for the obligations of
any other Finance Party under the Finance Documents.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">2.2.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The rights of each Finance Party under or in connection with
the Finance Documents are separate and independent rights and any
debt arising under the Finance Documents to a Finance Party from the
Obligors shall be a separate and independent debt.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">2.2.3</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>A Finance Party may, except as otherwise stated in the Finance
Documents, separately enforce its rights under the Finance Documents.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">3.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>PURPOSE</B></TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">3.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Purpose</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">The Borrower shall apply all amounts borrowed by it under the Facility
towards (i)&nbsp;the financing of the acquisition and development of the New
Fields, (ii)&nbsp;the financing of the development of the Existing Fields,
(iii)&nbsp;general corporate purposes (including payment of fees and expenses
incurred under this Agreement) and/or (iv)&nbsp;the development by the Group of
hydrocarbon fields in Turkey.


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">3.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Monitoring</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">No Finance Party is bound to monitor or verify the application of any
amount borrowed pursuant to this Agreement, however the Agent shall have
the right to request from the Borrower evidence that the Loans are applied
to the purposes mentioned in Clause 3.1 <I>Purpose</I>).


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">- 18 -

</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 4%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">The Borrower may draw a Loan by delivery to the Agent of a duly completed
Utilisation Request not later than 3.00 p.m. (Paris time) three (3)
Business Days prior to the proposed Utilisation Date. No Utilisation
Request shall be sent in respect of the portion of a Loan which is
automatically rolled over in accordance with Clause 7.1 (<I>Repayment</I>).

Base Determination Date to the Reserve Tail Date divided by</TD>

twenty-one (21)&nbsp;Business Days before each Borrowing Base

Base Reduction Schedule at least fifteen (15)&nbsp;Business Days before

deemed to have given their consent to such Borrowing Base and
Borrowing Base Reduction Schedule if they have not answered to the

relevant Borrowing Base Determination Date.</TD>

    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">6.2.6</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>If (i)&nbsp;all the Lenders, as far as an increase of the Borrowing
Base (and the determination of a new Borrowing Base Reduction
Schedule accordingly) is concerned or (ii)&nbsp;the Majority Lenders, as
far as a decrease of the Borrowing Base (and the determination of a
new Borrowing Base Reduction Schedule accordingly) is</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>concerned, cannot reach an agreement as to the re-determination of
the Borrowing Base and the new Borrowing Base Reduction Schedule at
least fifteen (15)&nbsp;Business Days before the relevant Borrowing Base
Determination Date, all the Lenders shall meet in order to approve,
at the latest ten (10)&nbsp;Business Days before the relevant Borrowing
Base Determination Date, the new Borrowing Base and new Borrowing
Base Reduction Schedule (provided that the Lenders shall decide in
accordance with the majority or unanimity stipulated in paragraph
6.2.4 (a)&nbsp;and (b)&nbsp;above). Should the Lenders fail to reach an

Borrowing Base Determination Date, the Technical Bank shall appoint
the Determination Lender(s) at the latest eight (8)&nbsp;Business Days
before the relevant Borrowing Base Determination Date. The
Determination Lender(s) shall deliver to the Technical Bank its
(their)&nbsp;proposal as the applicable Borrowing Base and Borrowing
Base Reduction Schedule, as calculated in accordance with
paragraphs 6.2.1 and 6.2.2, at the latest five (5)&nbsp;Business Days
before the relevant Borrowing Base Determination Date. The
applicable Borrowing Base and Borrowing Base Reduction Schedule
shall be determined conclusively as being the average Borrowing
Base and Borrowing Base Reduction Schedule proposed by the three
Determination Lender(s). Such Borrowing Base and Borrowing Base
Reduction Schedule shall be binding on the Borrowers and the
Finance Parties.</TD>
</TR>

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Borrowing Base Deficiency</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>If on any Borrowing Base Determination Date, the amount standing to the
credit of the Collection Account is not sufficient to repay to the Agent
the amount of the Borrowing Base Deficiency, the Borrower shall have a
sixty (60)&nbsp;days grace period to (a)&nbsp;repay to the Agent the amount
necessary to ensure that the Outstanding Amount does not exceed the
Maximum Amount or (b)&nbsp;validly create a cash collateral (<I>gage-esp&#232;ces</I>) or
other Encumbrance satisfactory to the Finance Parties, for an amount at
least equal to the amount of Borrowing Base Deficiency. If, at the expiry
of this sixty (60)&nbsp;days grace period after the Borrowing Base Deficiency
has been established, the Outstanding Amount exceeds the Maximum Amount or
no satisfactory cash collateral (<I>gage-esp&#232;ces</I>) or other Encumbrance has
been validly created in favour of the Finance Parties, the Lenders shall
be entitled to exercise any of their rights under this Agreement,
including, without limitation, to declare all amounts accrued or
outstanding under the Finance Documents immediately due and payable in
accordance with Clause 23.1(a) (<I>Non-payment</I>) and 23.19 (<I>Acceleration</I>).</TD>
</TR>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>SECTION 4<BR>
REPAYMENT, PREPAYMENT AND CANCELLATION</B>



<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>REPAYMENT</B></TD>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Repayment of Loans</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Borrower shall repay each Loan on each Reduction Date. However the
consolidated Loan (in accordance with Clause 10.3 (<I>Consolidation of
Loans</I>)) will be deemed automatically rolled over (in the same amount or in
an amount determined in accordance with Clause 7.2 <I>(Reduction of the
Facility</I>), as the case may be) on each Reduction Date, until the Final
Maturity Date.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">

</TR>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">7.2.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>On each Reduction Date, unless the Outstanding Amount is
already equal to or less than the Maximum Amount (taking into account
the reduction on that day of the Borrowing Base in accordance with
the Borrowing Base Reduction Schedule), the Borrower shall ensure
that sufficient Loans are repaid on that Reduction Date to the extent
necessary so that the Outstanding Amount (after that repayment) is
equal to or less than the reduced amount of the Maximum Amount (as
calculated on that Reduction Date).</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Reduction Instalment shall be paid by the Borrower on each
Reduction Date in accordance with the provisions of Clause 29.1
(<I>Payments by the Borrower</I>).</TD>
</TR>

    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Any reduction of the Outstanding Amount shall reduce rateably
the participation of each Lender in the Loans.</TD>

</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">

with Schedule&nbsp;3 (<I>Maximum Facility Amount Amortization Schedule</I>) shall
reduce rateably the Commitments of the Lenders.</TD>

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Compliance with financial ratios</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 8%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">In the event that, on any Reduction Date, the LLCR is inferior to
1.15 and/or the DSCR is inferior to 1.10 and/or the ALCR is
inferior to 1.25, each as calculated on the latest Ratio
Calculation Date, the Reduction Instalment to be paid by the
Borrower on such Reduction Date shall be increased up to the amount
as shall be necessary to ensure that the LLCR is at least equal to
1.15, the DSCR is at least equal to 1.10 and the ALCR is at least
equal to 1.25 on that Reduction Date.

Borrower shall repay that Lender&#146;s participation in that Loan.</TD>

    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">9.3.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>If (i)&nbsp;the Borrower fails to pay any amount payable by it
under a Finance Document on its due date, interest shall accrue to
the fullest extent permitted by law on the overdue amount from the
due date up to the date of actual payment (both before and after
judgment) at a rate which, subject to paragraph (b)&nbsp;below, is 2%
higher than the rate which would have been payable if the overdue
amount had, during the period of non-payment, constituted a Loan for
successive Interest Periods, each of a duration selected by the Agent
(acting reasonably). Any interest accruing under this Clause 9.3
shall be immediately payable by the Borrower on demand by the Agent.</TD>

be compounded with the overdue amount only if, within the meaning of
article 1154 of the French <I>Code Civil</I>, such interest is due for a
period of at least one year, but will remain immediately due and
payable.</TD>

    <TD>Interest Periods</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">10.1.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The duration of each Interest Period is one (1)&nbsp;Month. The duration
of an Interest Period shall be shortened (i)&nbsp;in order to ensure that
the last day of each Interest Period corresponds to a Reduction Date
or (ii)&nbsp;for the purpose of consolidation of Loans as provided in
Clause 10.3 (<I>Consolidation of Loans</I>), in which case the applicable
rate of interest on such Loan for that Interest Period shall be the
percentage rate per annum which is the aggregate of the applicable
(i)&nbsp;Margin, (ii)&nbsp;the market rate (<I>taux de march&#233;</I>) as determined by
the Agent and (iii)&nbsp;Mandatory Cost, if any.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">10.1.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>A Loan has one Interest Period only and each Loan will be deemed
automatically rolled over on each Reduction Date up to an amount
equal to (a)&nbsp;the Outstanding Amount on such Reduction Date minus (b)
the aggregate of the Reduction Instalment and any amount to be repaid
in accordance with Clause 8 (<I>Prepayment and Cancellation</I>).</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">10.1.3</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>No Interest Period for any Loan shall extend beyond the Final
Maturity Date. If an Interest Period would otherwise extend beyond
the Final Maturity Date, it shall be shortened so that it ends on the
Final Maturity Date.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>before close of business in Paris two (2)
Business Days prior to the proposed Utilisation Date, the
Agent receives notifications from a Lender or Lenders (whose
participations in a Loan exceed thirty-five (35)&nbsp;per cent.
(35%) of that Loan) that the cost to it of obtaining matching
deposits in the Relevant Interbank Market would be in excess
of LIBOR.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">11.3</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Alternative basis of interest or funding</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">11.3.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>If a Market Disruption Event occurs and the Agent or the Borrower
so requires, the Agent and the Borrower shall enter into negotiations
(for a period of not more than forty five (45)&nbsp;days) with a view to
agreeing a substitute basis for determining the rate of interest.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">11.3.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Any alternative basis agreed pursuant to paragraph (a)&nbsp;above shall,
with the prior consent of all the Lenders and the Borrower, be
binding on all Parties.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">11.4</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Break Costs</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">11.4.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Borrower shall, within three (3)&nbsp;Business Days of demand by a
Finance Party, pay to that Finance Party its Break Costs attributable
to all or any part of a Loan or Unpaid Sum being paid by the Borrower
on a day other than the last day of an Interest Period for that Loan
or Unpaid Sum.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">11.4.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Each Lender shall, as soon as reasonably practicable after a demand
by the Agent, provide a certificate confirming the calculation of the
amount of its Break Costs for any Interest Period in which they
accrue.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">12.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>FEES</B></TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">12.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Commitment fee</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">- 30 -
</DIV>

</TABLE>

<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">12.1.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>

Lender) a commitment fee computed at the rate of 50% of the Margin
then applicable on the Available Amount.</TD>

    <TD>The accrued commitment fee is payable monthly in arrears on each
Reduction Date.</TD>
</TR>

<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

stipulated in the Fee Letter.</TD>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>SECTION 6<BR>
ADDITIONAL PAYMENT OBLIGATIONS</B>



<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>TAX GROSS UP AND INDEMNITIES</B></TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Definitions</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.1.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>In this Agreement:</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>&#147;<B>Protected Party</B>&#148; means a Finance Party which is or will be subject
to any liability, or required to make any payment, for or on
account of Tax in relation to a sum received or receivable (or any
sum deemed for the purposes of Tax to be received or receivable)
under a Finance Document.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>&#147;<B>Qualifying Lender</B>&#148; means a Lender which:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>has its Facility Office in France; or</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>fulfils the conditions imposed by French Law
taking into account, as the case may be, any double taxation
agreement (subject to the completion of any necessary
procedural formalities), in order for a payment not to be
subject to (or as the case may be, to be exempt from) any Tax
Deduction.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>&#147;<B>Tax Credit</B>&#148; means a credit against, relief or remission for, or
repayment of any Tax.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>&#147;<B>Tax Deduction</B>&#148; means a deduction or withholding for or on account
of Tax from a payment under a Finance Document.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>&#147;<B>Tax Payment</B>&#148; means an increased payment made by an Obligor to a
Finance Party under Clause 13.2 (<I>Tax gross-up</I>) or a payment under
Clause 13.3 (<I>Tax indemnity</I>).</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>&#147;<B>Treaty Lender</B>&#148; means a Lender which is entitled to a payment under
a double taxation agreement (subject to the completion of any
necessary procedural formalities) without a Tax Deduction.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.1.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Unless a contrary indication appears, in this Clause 13 a reference
to &#147;determines&#148; or &#147;determined&#148; means a determination made in the
absolute discretion of the person making the determination.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Tax gross-up</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.2.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Each Obligor shall make all payments to be made by it without any
Tax Deduction, unless a Tax Deduction is required by law.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.2.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Each Obligor shall promptly upon becoming aware that it must make a
Tax Deduction (or that there is any change in the rate or the basis
of a Tax Deduction) notify the Agent accordingly. Similarly, a Lender
shall notify the Agent on becoming so aware in respect of a payment
payable to that Lender. If the Agent receives such notification from
a Lender it shall notify the relevant Obligor.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">- 32 -
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">


<P><TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">


<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.2.3</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>If a Tax Deduction is required by law to be made by an Obligor, the
amount of the payment due from that Obligor shall be increased to an
amount which (after making any Tax Deduction) leaves an amount equal
to the payment which would have been due if no Tax Deduction had been
required.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.2.4</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>That Obligor is not required to make an increased payment to a
Lender under paragraph 13.2.3 above for a Tax Deduction in respect of
tax imposed by France from a payment of interest on a Loan, if on the
date on which the payment falls due:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the payment could have been made to the relevant
Lender without a Tax Deduction if it was a Qualifying Lender,
but on that date that Lender is not or has ceased to be a
Qualifying Lender other than as a result of any change after
the date it became a Lender under this Agreement in (or in the
interpretation, administration, or application of) any law or
double taxation agreement, or any published practice or
concession of any relevant taxing authority; or</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the relevant Lender is a Treaty Lender and the
Obligor making the payment is able to demonstrate that the
payment could have been made to the Lender without the Tax
Deduction had that Lender complied with its obligations under
paragraph 13.2.7 below.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.2.5</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>If an Obligor is required to make a Tax Deduction, that Obligor
shall make that Tax Deduction and any payment required in connection
with that Tax Deduction within the time allowed and in the minimum
amount required by law.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.2.6</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Within thirty (30)&nbsp;Business Days of making either a Tax Deduction
or any payment required in connection with that Tax Deduction, the
Obligor making that Tax Deduction shall deliver to the Agent for the
Finance Party entitled to the payment evidence reasonably
satisfactory to that Finance Party that the Tax Deduction has been
made or (as applicable) any appropriate payment paid to the relevant
taxing authority.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.2.7</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>A Treaty Lender and the Obligor which makes a payment to which that
Treaty Lender is entitled shall co-operate in completing any
procedural formalities necessary for that Obligor to obtain
authorisation to make that payment without a Tax Deduction.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.3</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Tax indemnity</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.3.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Each Obligor shall (within three (3)&nbsp;Business Days of demand by the
Agent) pay to a Protected Party an amount equal to the loss,
liability or cost which that Protected Party determines (on the basis
of justification to be communicated to the Borrower at his reasonable
request) will be or has been (directly or indirectly) suffered for or
on account of Tax by that Protected Party in respect of a Finance
Document.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.3.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Paragraph&nbsp;13.3.1 above shall not apply:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>with respect to any Tax assessed on a Finance
Party:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="13%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(i)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>under the law of the jurisdiction in
which that Finance Party is incorporated or, if
different, the jurisdiction (or jurisdictions) in which
that Finance Party is treated as resident for tax
purposes; or</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">- 33 -
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">


<P><TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">


<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="13%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(ii)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>under the law of the jurisdiction in
which that Finance Party&#146;s Facility Office is located in
respect of amounts received or receivable in that
jurisdiction,</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>if that Tax is imposed on or calculated by reference to the
net income received or receivable (but not any sum deemed to
be received or receivable) by that Finance Party; or</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>to the extent a loss, liability or cost:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="13%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(i)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>is compensated for by an increased
payment under Clause 13.2 (<I>Tax gross-up</I>); or</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="13%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(ii)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>would have been compensated for by an
increased payment under Clause 13.2 (<I>Tax gross-up</I>) but
was not so compensated solely because one of the
exclusions in paragraph 13.2.4 applied.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.3.3</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>A Protected Party making, or intending to make a claim under
paragraph (a)&nbsp;above shall promptly notify the Agent of the event
which will give, or has given, rise to the claim, following which the
Agent shall notify the relevant Obligor.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.3.4</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>A Protected Party shall, on receiving a payment from the relevant
Obligor under this Clause 13.3, notify the Agent.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>If an Obligor makes a Tax Payment and the relevant Finance Party determines that:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">

    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.4.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>a Tax Credit is attributable to that Tax Payment; and</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.4.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>that Finance Party has obtained, utilised and retained that Tax Credit,</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the Finance Party shall pay an amount to that Obligor which that Finance
Party determines will leave it (after that payment) in the same after-Tax
position as it would have been in had the Tax Payment not been made by
that Obligor.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>

    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Borrower shall pay and, within three Business Days of demand,
indemnify each Finance Party against any cost, loss or liability that
Finance Party incurs in relation to all stamp duty, registration and other
similar Taxes payable in respect of any Finance Document.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.6</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Value added tax</TD>
</TR>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">13.6.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>All consideration expressed to be payable under a Finance Document
by any Party to a Finance Party shall be deemed to be exclusive of
any VAT. If VAT is chargeable, on any supply made by any Finance
Party to any Party in connection with a Finance Document, that Party
shall pay to the Finance Party (in addition to and at the same time
as paying the consideration) an amount equal to the amount of the
VAT.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">16.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>MITIGATION BY THE LENDERS</B></TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">16.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Mitigation</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">16.1.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Each Finance Party shall, in consultation with the Borrower, take
all reasonable steps to mitigate any circumstances which arise and
which would result in any amount becoming payable under or pursuant
to, or cancelled pursuant to, any of Clause 8.1 (<I>Illegality</I>), Clause
13 (<I>Tax gross up and indemnities</I>) Clause 14 (<I>Increased costs</I>) or
Schedule&nbsp;5 (<I>Mandatory Cost Formulae</I>) including (but not limited to)
transferring its rights and obligations under the Finance Documents
to another Affiliate or Facility Office in a manner which would avoid
or minimize the circumstances in question and on terms acceptable to
the Agent and the Lenders.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">16.1.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Paragraph&nbsp;16.1.1 above does not in any way limit the obligations of
the Obligors under the Finance Documents.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">16.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Limitation of liability</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">16.2.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Borrower shall indemnify each Finance Party for all costs and
expenses reasonably incurred by that Finance Party as a result of
steps taken by it under Clause 16.1 (Mitigation).</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">16.2.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>A Finance Party is not obliged to take any steps under Clause 16.1
(<I>Mitigation</I>) if, in the opinion of that Finance Party (acting
reasonably), to do so might be prejudicial to it.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

    <TD>promptly and in any event within fifteen (15)&nbsp;days after the U.S.

ERISA Event which, individually or when aggregated with any other

Effect has occurred, a written statement describing such ERISA Event
and the action, if any, which such U.S. Obligor or Affiliate proposes
to take with respect to such ERISA Event and a copy of any notice
filed with the PBGC or the IRS pertaining to such ERISA Event.</TD>

Business Day) (each such date being a Ratio Calculation Date). Such
ratios shall be sent by the Agent to the Lenders for approval by the
Majority Lenders fifteen (15)&nbsp;Business Days before such Ratio
Calculation Date. If Lenders representing more than the Majority
Lenders notify in writing their disagreement with the ratios
calculated by the Agent (such notification to be received by the
Agent at least ten (10)&nbsp;Business Days before the relevant Ratio
Calculation Determination Date), all the Lenders shall meet in order
to approve (on the basis of the decision of the Majority Lenders), at
the latest five (5)&nbsp;Business Days before the relevant Ratio
Calculation Date, the ALCR, LLCR and DSCR. Should the Lenders fail
to reach an agreement at the latest five (5)&nbsp;Business</TD>

for Brent future (as determined by the London International
Petroleum Exchange (&#147;<B>IPE</B>&#148;) falls below (i)&nbsp;28 USD per barrel
for the year 2005, (ii)&nbsp;26 USD per barrel for the year 2006
and (iii)&nbsp;25 USD per barrel for the years thereafter, the
Borrower shall promptly enter into and maintain at any time
thereafter Hedge Agreements (complying with requirements
provided in paragraphs (b)&nbsp;to (e)&nbsp;above) in relation to
Petroleum covering in aggregate at least 60% of the Borrower
(and its Subsidiaries) estimated monthly production of crude
oil from the PDP Reserves during the next 12&nbsp;months as
determined by the Technical Bank on each Borrowing Base
Determination Date. Such Hedge Agreements will maintain the
Borrowing Base and shall be in terms reasonably satisfactory
to the Agent.</TD>

</TR>

    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>waives any rights of recourse prior to payment (<I>recours avant
paiement</I>) against the Borrower under article 2032 of the French <I>Code
civil</I>; and</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">22.3.4</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>waives any rights under article 2039 of the French <I>Code civil </I>to
take any action against the Borrower in the event of any extension of
the final repayment date of the Guaranteed Obligations or any other
date for payment of any amount due, owing or payable to any Finance
Party under any Guaranteed Obligation, even if decided without the
consent of the Guarantor, agrees that the guarantee will remain in
full force and effect notwithstanding such extension and acknowledges
that it will remain bound by the original maturity date of the
Guaranteed Obligations.</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">23.6</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Insolvency</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">23.6.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>A member of the Group is unable or admits inability pursuant to any
insolvency proceedings to pay its debts as they fall due, suspends
making payments on any of its debts or, by reason of actual or
anticipated financial difficulties, commences negotiations with one
or more of its creditors with a view to rescheduling any of its
indebtedness.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">23.6.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>An Obligor or any member of the Group is in a state of <I>cessation
des paiements </I>or becomes insolvent for the purpose of any applicable
insolvency law.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">23.6.3</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>A moratorium is declared in respect of any indebtedness of any
member of the Group provided that such would have a Material Adverse
Effect.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

    <TD>Any corporate action, legal proceedings or other procedure or step
is taken in relation to:</TD>
</TR>

    <TD>the suspension of payments, a moratorium of any

</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">

    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(d)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>enforcement of any Encumbrance over any assets of
any member of the Group, exceeding in aggregate USD 500,000.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

l&#146;entreprise </I>or <I>liquidation judiciaire </I>is entered in relation to an

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">24.2.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Borrower shall ensure that, at any time after the Grace Period,

Balance.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">

    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">24.2.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>In addition to its obligations under paragraph 24.2.1 above, the
Borrower shall ensure that not later than three (3)&nbsp;Business Days
prior to each Reduction Date, the Collection Account Balance shall be
at least equal to the amount of the Loans, interest, fees, costs and
other sums due and payable on that Reduction Date, plus, after the
Grace Period, the Minimum Balance.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Borrower shall not be entitled to receive, withdraw or
otherwise transfer the Collection Account Balance (or any part
thereof) provided that, if, at any time:</TD>
</TR>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>all sums due on such date under the Finance
Documents, the Insurance Policy and the Hedge Agreements have
been irrevocably paid in full;</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>no Default shall have occurred and be continuing;</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(c)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the Loan Life Cover Ratio at the latest Ratio
Calculation Date is not less than 1.2;</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(d)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the Asset Life Cover Ratio at the latest Ratio
Calculation Date is not less than 1.3;</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(e)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>

Calculation Date is not less than 1.15;</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(f)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>no Borrowing Base Deficiency exists as at such
date which has not been remedied in accordance with Clause 6.4
(<I>Borrowing Base Deficiency</I>); and</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(g)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the Agent determines, in its absolute and sole
discretion, that the Borrower will be able to meet all of its
repayment obligations under this Agreement at the appropriate
time,</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P align="left" style="margin-left: 8%; text-indent: 0%; margin-right: 0%; font-size: 10pt">then the Agent shall transfer into the Borrower&#146;s current account
(of which the Collection Account is a sub-division) an amount equal
to the Collection Account Balance minus, after the Grace Period,
the Minimum Balance.
