<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>SECTION 8<BR>
CHANGES TO PARTIES</B>



<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">25.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>CHANGES TO THE LENDERS</B></TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">25.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Assignments and transfers by the Lenders</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">25.1.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Subject to this Clause 25, a Lender (the &#147;<B>Existing Lender</B>&#148;) may:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>assign any of its rights; or</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>transfer any of its rights (including such as
relate to that Lender&#146;s participation in each Loan) and
obligations,</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>to another bank or financial institution (the &#147;<B>New Lender</B>&#148;).</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">25.1.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The consent of the Finance Parties is hereby given to a transfer by
an Existing Lender to a New Lender.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">25.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Conditions of assignment or transfer</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">25.2.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The consent of the Borrower is required for an assignment or
transfer by a Lender, provided that:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>in the case of an assignment, no consent is
required if the assignment is to another Lender or an
Affiliate of a Lender, and</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the Borrower hereby consents to a transfer to
another Lender or an Affiliate of a Lender.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">25.2.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The consent of the Borrower to an assignment or transfer must not
be unreasonably withheld or delayed. The Borrower will be deemed to
have given its consent five (5)&nbsp;Business Days after the Lender has
requested it unless consent is expressly refused by the Borrower
within that time.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">25.2.3</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The consent of the Borrower to an assignment or transfer must not
be withheld solely because the assignment or transfer may result in
an increase to the Mandatory Cost.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">25.2.4</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>An assignment will only be effective as among the Finance Parties
on receipt by the Agent of written confirmation from the New Lender
(in form and substance satisfactory to the Agent) that the New Lender
has become entitled to the same rights and will assume the same
obligations to the other Finance Parties as it would have been under
if it was an Original Lender.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">25.2.5</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>A transfer will only be effective if the procedure set out in
Clause 25.4 (<I>Procedure for transfer</I>) is complied with.</TD>
</TR>


</TABLE>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">- 69 -

<P>

<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">25.4</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Procedure for transfer</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">25.4.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Subject to the conditions set out in Clause 25.2 (<I>Conditions of
assignment or transfer</I>) a transfer is effected in accordance with
paragraph 25.4.2 below when the Agent executes a duly completed
Transfer Agreement delivered to it by the Existing Lender and the New
Lender. The Agent shall, as soon as reasonably practicable after
receipt by it of a duly completed Transfer Agreement appearing on its
face to comply with the terms of this Agreement and delivered in
accordance with the terms of this Agreement, execute that Transfer
Agreement.</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">25.4.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>By virtue of the execution of a Transfer Agreement, as from the
Transfer Date:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>to the extent that in the Transfer Agreement the
Existing Lender seeks to transfer its rights and obligations
under the Finance Documents, the Existing Lender shall be
discharged to the extent provided for in the Transfer
Agreement from further obligations towards the Borrower and
the other Finance Parties under the Finance Documents;</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the rights and obligations of the Existing Lender
with respect to the Borrower shall be transferred to the New
Lender, to the extent provided for in the Transfer Agreement;</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(c)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the Agent, the Arranger, the New Lender and other
Lenders shall have the same rights and obligations between
themselves as they would have had had the New Lender been an
Original Lender with the rights and/or obligations to which it
is entitled and subject as a result of the transfer and to
that extent the Agent, the Arranger and the Existing Lender
shall each be released from further obligations to each other
under the Finance Documents; and</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="9%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(d)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the New Lender shall become a Party as a
&#147;<B>Lender</B>&#148;.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">25.5</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Disclosure of information</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Any Lender may disclose to any of its Affiliates and any other person:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">25.5.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>to (or through) whom that Lender assigns or transfers (or may
potentially assign or transfer) all or any of its rights and
obligations under this Agreement;</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">25.5.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>with (or through) whom that Lender enters into (or may potentially
enter into) any sub-participation in relation to, or any other
transaction under which payments are to be made by reference to, this
Agreement or the Obligors; or</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="5%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">25.5.3</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>to whom, and to the extent that, information is required to be
disclosed by any applicable law or regulation,</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">- 71 -
</DIV>

    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>any information about the Obligors, the Group and the Finance Documents as
that Lender shall consider appropriate.</TD>
</TR>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">


<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>SECTION 9<BR>
THE FINANCE PARTIES</B>



<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>ROLE OF THE AGENT, THE ARRANGER AND THE TECHNICAL BANK</B></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Appointment of the Agent</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.1.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Each other Finance Party appoints the Agent to act as its agent
under and in connection with the Finance Documents (including the
Security Documents).</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.1.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Each other Finance Party authorises the Agent to exercise the
rights, powers, authorities and discretions specifically given to the
Agent under or in connection with the Finance Documents (including
the Security Documents) together with any other incidental rights,
powers, authorities and discretions.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.1.3</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Each other Finance Party authorises in advance the Agent to sign in
its name and on its behalf all Security Documents and any other
document in connection with the Security Documents whether at the
time of execution, enforcement or release of the Security created
pursuant thereto or at any other time and any document relating to
the enforcement of the Security Documents.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Duties of the Agent</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.2.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Agent shall promptly forward to a Party the original or a copy
of any document which is delivered to the Agent for that Party by any
other Party.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.2.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Except where a Finance Document specifically provides otherwise,
the Agent is not obliged to review or check the adequacy, accuracy or
completeness of any document it forwards to another Party.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.2.3</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>If the Agent receives notice from a Party referring to this
Agreement, describing a Default and stating that the circumstance
described is a Default, it shall promptly notify the Finance Parties.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.2.4</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>If the Agent is aware of the non-payment of any principal,
interest, commitment fee or other fee payable to a Finance Party
(other than the Agent, the Arranger or the Technical Bank) under
this Agreement it shall promptly notify the other Finance Parties.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.2.5</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Agent&#146;s duties under the Finance Documents are solely
mechanical and administrative in nature.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.3</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Role of the Arranger and the Technical Bank<BR><BR>
Except as specifically provided in the Finance Documents, the Arranger,
and the Technical Bank have no obligations of any kind to any other Party
under or in connection with any Finance Document.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">- 73 -
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">


<P><TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">


<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.4</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>No fiduciary duties</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.4.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Nothing in this Agreement constitutes the Agent, the Arranger or
the Technical Bank as a trustee or fiduciary of any other person.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.4.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Neither the Agent nor the Technical Bank nor the Arranger shall be
bound to account to any Lender for any sum or the profit element of
any sum received by it for its own account.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.5</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Business with the Group<BR><BR>
The Agent, the Arranger and the Technical Bank may accept deposits from,
lend money to and generally engage in any kind of banking or other
business with any member of the Group.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.6</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Rights and discretions of the Agent</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.6.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Agent may rely on:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="12%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>any representation, notice or document believed
by it to be genuine, correct and appropriately authorised; and</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="12%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>any statement made by a director, authorised
signatory or employee of any person regarding any matters
which may reasonably be assumed to be within his knowledge or
within his power to verify.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.6.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Agent may assume (unless it has received notice to the contrary
in its capacity as agent for the Lenders) that:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="12%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>no Default has occurred (unless it has actual
knowledge of a Default arising under Clause 23.1
(<I>Non-payment</I>)); and</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="12%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>any right, power, authority or discretion vested
in any Party or the Majority Lenders has not been exercised.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.6.3</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Agent may engage, pay for and rely on the advice or services of
any lawyers, accountants, surveyors or other experts.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.6.4</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Agent may act in relation to the Finance Documents through its
personnel and agents.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.6.5</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Agent may disclose to any other Party any information it
reasonably believes it has received as agent under this Agreement.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.6.6</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Notwithstanding any other provision of any Finance Document to the
contrary, neither the Agent nor the Technical Bank or the Arranger is
obliged to do or omit to do anything if it would or might in its
reasonable opinion constitute a breach of any law or regulation or a
breach of a fiduciary duty or duty of confidentiality.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.7</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Majority Lenders&#146; instructions</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.7.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Unless a contrary indication appears in a Finance Document, the
Agent shall exercise any right, power, authority or discretion vested
in it as Agent in accordance with any</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">- 74 -
</DIV>

<!-- PAGEBREAK -->
<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">


<P><TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">
<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #textcolor#; background: #bgcolor#">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>instructions given to it by the Majority Lenders (or, if so
instructed by the Majority Lenders, refrain from exercising any
right, power, authority or discretion vested in it as Agent) and
(b)&nbsp;not be liable for any act (or omission) if it acts (or refrains
from taking any action) in accordance with an instruction of the
Majority Lenders.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.7.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Unless a contrary indication appears in a Finance Document, any
instructions given by the Majority Lenders will be binding on all the
Finance Parties.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.7.3</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Agent may refrain from acting in accordance with the
instructions of the Majority Lenders (or, if appropriate, the
Lenders) until it has received such security as it may require for
any cost, loss or liability (together with any associated VAT) which
it may incur in complying with the instructions.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.7.4</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>In the absence of instructions from the Majority Lenders, (or, if
appropriate, the Lenders) the Agent may act (or refrain from taking
action) as it considers to be in the best interest of the Lenders.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.7.5</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Agent is not authorised to act on behalf of a Lender in any
legal or arbitration proceedings relating to any Finance Document,
without having first obtained that Lender&#146;s authority to act on its
behalf in those proceedings.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.8</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Responsibility for documentation<BR><BR>
Neither the Agent, the Arranger nor the Technical Bank:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.8.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>is responsible for the adequacy, accuracy and/or completeness of
any information (whether oral or written) supplied by the Agent, the
Arranger, the Obligors or any other person given in or in connection
with any Finance Document; or</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.8.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>is responsible for the legality, validity, effectiveness, adequacy
or enforceability of any Finance Document or any other agreement,
arrangement or document entered into, made or executed in
anticipation of or in connection with any Finance Document.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.9</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Exclusion of liability</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.9.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Without limiting paragraph 27.9.2 below, the Agent or the Technical
Bank will not be liable for any action taken by it under or in
connection with any Finance Document, unless directly caused by its
gross negligence or wilful misconduct.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.9.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>No Party may take any proceedings against any officer, employee or
agent of the Agent or the Technical Bank in respect of any claim it
might have against the Agent or the Technical Bank or in respect of
any act or omission of any kind by that officer, employee or agent in
relation to any Finance Document and any officer, employee or agent
of the Agent or the Technical Bank may rely on this Clause 27.9.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.9.3</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Agent will not be liable for any delay (or any related
consequences) in crediting an account with an amount required under
the Finance Documents to be paid by the Agent if the Agent has taken
all necessary steps as soon as reasonably practicable to comply with
the regulations or operating procedures of any recognised clearing or
settlement system used by the Agent for that purpose.
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">- 75 -

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.10</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Lenders&#146; indemnity to the Agent and the Technical Bank<BR><BR>
Each Lender shall (in proportion to its share of the Total Commitments or,
if the Total Commitments are then zero, to its share of the Total
Commitments immediately prior to their reduction to zero) indemnify the
Agent and the Technical Bank, within three Business Days of demand,
against any cost, loss or liability incurred by the Agent and the
Technical Bank (otherwise than by reason of the Agent&#146;s or the Technical
Bank&#146;s gross negligence or wilful misconduct) in acting as Agent or
Technical Bank under the Finance Documents (unless they have been
reimbursed by the Borrower pursuant to a Finance Document).</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.11</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Resignation of the Agent or the Technical Bank</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.11.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Agent may resign and appoint one of its Affiliates as
successor by giving notice to the other Finance Parties and the
Borrower.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.11.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Alternatively the Agent may resign by giving notice to the other
Finance Parties and the Borrower, in which case the Majority Lenders
(after consultation with the Borrower) may appoint a successor Agent.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.11.3</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>If the Majority Lenders have not appointed a successor Agent in
accordance with paragraph (b)&nbsp;above within 30&nbsp;days after notice of
resignation was given, the Agent (after consultation with the
Borrower) may appoint a successor Agent.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.11.4</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The retiring Agent shall, at its own cost, make available to the
successor Agent such documents and records and provide such
assistance as the successor Agent may reasonably request for the
purposes of performing its functions as Agent under the Finance
Documents.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.11.5</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Agent&#146;s resignation notice shall only take effect upon the
appointment of a successor.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.11.6</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Upon the appointment of a successor, the retiring Agent shall be
discharged from any further obligation in respect of the Finance
Documents but shall remain entitled to the benefit of this Clause 27.
Its successor and each of the other Parties shall have the same
rights and obligations amongst themselves as they would have had if
such successor had been an original Party.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.11.7</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Technical Bank may resign in the same conditions as the Agent,
as provided in this Clause 27.11.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Confidentiality</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>

    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.12.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>In acting as agent for the Finance Parties, the Agent shall be
regarded as acting through its agency division which shall be treated
as a separate entity from any other of its divisions or departments.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>If information is received by another division or department of
the Agent, it may be treated as confidential to that division or
department and the Agent shall not be deemed to have notice of it.
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>

including but not limited to:</TD>

    <TD>the financial condition, status and nature of each member of the
Group;</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

    <TD>the legality, validity, effectiveness, adequacy or enforceability
of any Finance Document and any other agreement, arrangement or

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">27.15</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Deduction from amounts payable by the Agent<BR><BR>
If any Party owes an amount to the Agent under the Finance Documents the
Agent may, after giving notice to that Party, deduct an amount not
exceeding that amount from any payment to that Party which the Agent would
otherwise be obliged to make under the Finance Documents and apply the
amount deducted in or towards satisfaction of the amount owed. For the
purposes of the Finance Documents that Party shall be regarded as having
received any amount so deducted.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>CONDUCT OF BUSINESS BY THE FINANCE PARTIES</B><BR><BR>
No provision of this Agreement will:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

affairs (tax or otherwise) in whatever manner it thinks fit;</TD>

relief, remission or repayment available to it or the extent, order
and manner of any claim; or</TD>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>SECTION 10<BR>
ADMINISTRATION</B>



<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">29.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>PAYMENT MECHANICS</B></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">29.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Payments by the Borrower</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">29.1.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>On each date on which such sums are due under a Finance Document,
the Agent (acting on behalf of the Lenders) will apply any amount
standing to the credit of the Collection Account to:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="12%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the payment of any unpaid fees, costs and
expenses due under this Agreement or the Fee Letter;</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="12%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the payment of any sums, to be repaid in
accordance with the provisions of Clause 8 (<I>Prepayment and
Cancellation</I>); and</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="12%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(c)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the payment of any other sums due to the Finance
Parties under the Finance Documents, including any Reduction
Instalment.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">29.1.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Borrower agrees that in the event it fails to do so, the Agent
may at any time debit the Collection Account to pay the premiums due
under the Insurance Policy and the fees, costs, deposits and margin
calls due under the Hedge Agreements.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">29.1.3</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Borrower expressly and irrevocably authorises the Agent (acting
on behalf of the Lenders) to debit the Collection Account for the
purpose of payment of the sums mentioned in paragraphs 29.1.1, 29.1.2
and 29.1.3 above.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">29.1.4</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>In the event that on any date on which a payment must be made under
the Finance Documents the sums standing to the credit of the
Collection Account are not sufficient to pay in full all sums due on
that date, the Agent shall be entitled to recover the unpaid sums
directly from the Borrower.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">29.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Partial payments<BR><BR>
If, at any time, the Collection Account Balance is insufficient to
discharge all the amounts then due and payable under the Finance Documents
or the Insurance Policy, the Agent shall apply the Collection Account
Balance towards the obligations of the Borrower in the following order:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">29.2.1</TD>

<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">


<P><TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">


<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>lastly</B>, in or towards payment of any other sum due but unpaid under
the Finance Documents.</TD>
</TR>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">29.3</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Payments to the Agent<BR><BR>
On each date on which an Obligor or a Lender is required to make a payment
under a Finance Document, the Obligor or Lender shall make the same
available to the Agent (unless a contrary indication appears in a Finance
Document) for value on the due date at the time and in such funds
specified by the Agent as being customary at the time for settlement of
transactions in the relevant currency in the place of payment.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">29.4</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Clawback</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">29.4.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Where a sum is to be paid to the Agent under the Finance Documents
for another Party, the Agent is not obliged to pay that sum to that
other Party (or to enter into or perform any related exchange
contract) until it has been able to establish to its satisfaction
that it has actually received that sum.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">29.4.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>If the Agent pays an amount to another Party and it proves to be
the case that the Agent had not actually received that amount, then
the Party to whom that amount (or the proceeds of any related
exchange contract) was paid by the Agent shall on demand refund the
same to the Agent together with interest on that amount from the date
of payment to the date of receipt by the Agent, calculated by the
Agent to reflect its cost of funds.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">29.5</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>No set-off by Obligors<BR><BR>
All payments to be made by the Obligors under the Finance Documents shall
be calculated and be made without (and free and clear of any deduction
for) set-off or counterclaim.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">29.6</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Business Days</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">29.6.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Any payment which is due to be made on a day that is not a Business
Day shall be made on the next Business Day in the same calendar month
(if there is one) or the preceding Business Day (if there is not).</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">29.6.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>During any extension of the due date for payment of any principal
or an Unpaid Sum under this Agreement interest is payable on the
principal or Unpaid Sum at the rate payable on the original due date.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">29.7</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Currency of account</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="6%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">29.7.1</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Subject to paragraphs 29.7.2 to 29.7.5 below, USD and EUR are the
currencies of account and payment for any sum due from the Borrower
under any Finance Document.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>A repayment of a Loan or Unpaid Sum or a part of a Loan or Unpaid
Sum shall be made in the currency in which that Loan or Unpaid Sum is
denominated on its due date.
</TD>
</TR>

<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">30.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>SET-OFF</B><BR><BR>
A Finance Party may set off any matured obligation due from the Obligors
under the Finance Documents (to the extent beneficially owned by that
Finance Party) against any matured obligation owed by that Finance Party
to the Borrower, regardless of the place of payment, booking branch or
currency of either obligation. If the obligations are in different
currencies, the Finance Party may convert either obligation at a market
rate of exchange in its usual course of business for the purpose of the
set-off.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Accounts<BR><BR>
In any litigation or arbitration proceedings arising out of or in

<P><HR noshade><P>
<H5 align="left" style="page-break-before:always">&nbsp;</H5><P>

<DIV style="font-family: 'Times New Roman',Times,serif">


<P><TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">


<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">32.2</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Certificates and Determinations<BR><BR>
Any certification or determination by a Finance Party of a rate or amount
under any Finance Document is, in the absence of manifest error, <I>prima
facie </I>evidence of the matters to which it relates.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">32.3</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Day count convention<BR><BR>
Any interest, commission or fee accruing under a Finance Document will
accrue from day to day and is calculated on the basis of the actual number
of days elapsed and a year of 360&nbsp;days or, in any case where the practice
in the Relevant Interbank Market differs, in accordance with that market
practice.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">33.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>PARTIAL INVALIDITY</B><BR><BR>
If, at any time, any provision of the Finance Documents is or becomes
illegal, invalid or unenforceable in any respect under any law of any
jurisdiction, neither the legality, validity or enforceability of the
remaining provisions nor the legality, validity or enforceability of such
provision under the law of any other jurisdiction will in any way be
affected or impaired.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">34.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>REMEDIES AND WAIVERS</B><BR><BR>
No failure to exercise, nor any delay in exercising, on the part of any
Finance Party, any right or remedy under the Finance Documents shall
operate as a waiver, nor shall any single or partial exercise of any right
or remedy prevent any further or other exercise or the exercise of any
other right or remedy. The rights and remedies provided in this Agreement
are cumulative and not exclusive of any rights or remedies provided by
law.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">35.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD><B>CONSENTS, AMENDMENTS AND WAIVERS</B></TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>

    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Subject to Clause 35.2 (<I>Exceptions</I>) any term of the Finance

no Finance Party shall be prevented from taking proceedings relating to a
Dispute in any other courts with jurisdiction. To the extent allowed by
law, the Finance Parties may take concurrent proceedings in any number of
jurisdictions.</TD>
</TR>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt"><B>Schedule&nbsp;5<BR>
Mandatory Cost Formulae</B>



<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">1.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Mandatory Cost is an addition to the interest rate to compensate
Lenders for the cost of compliance with the requirements of the European
Central Bank.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">2.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>On the first day of each Interest Period (or as soon as possible
thereafter), the Agent shall calculate the Mandatory Cost, as a percentage
rate per annum, as a weighted average of the Lenders&#146; Additional Cost
Rates (as defined below) (weighted in proportion to the percentage
participation of each Lender in the relevant Loan).</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">3.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Each Lender lending from a Facility Office in a Participating Member
State will notify to the Agent its reasonable determination of the cost
(expressed as a percentage of that Lender&#146;s participation in all Loans
made from that Facility Office) of complying with the minimum reserve
requirements of the European Central Bank in respect of loans made from
that Facility Office (the &#147;<B>Additional Cost Rate</B>&#148;).</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">4.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Each Lender shall supply any information required by the Agent for the
purpose of calculating the Mandatory Cost. In particular, but without
limitation, each Lender shall supply the following information on or prior
to the date on which it becomes a Lender:</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(a)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>the jurisdiction of its Facility Office; and</TD>
</TR>

<TR>
    <TD colspan="5">&nbsp;</TD>
</TR>

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="3%" style="background: transparent">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">(b)</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>any other information that the Agent may reasonably require for
such purpose.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Each Lender shall promptly notify the Agent of any change to the
information provided by it pursuant to this paragraph.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">5.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Agent shall have no liability to any person if such determination
results in a Mandatory Cost which over or under compensates any Lender and
shall be entitled to assume that the information provided by any Lender
pursuant to paragraphs 3 and 4 above is true and correct in all respects.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">6.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Agent shall distribute the additional amounts received as a result of
the Mandatory Cost to the Lenders on the basis of the Additional Cost Rate
for each Lender based on the information provided by each Lender pursuant
to paragraphs 3 and 4 above.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">7.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>Any determination by the Agent pursuant to this Schedule in relation to a
formula, the Mandatory Cost, or any amount payable to a Lender shall, in
the absence of manifest error, be conclusive and binding on all Parties.</TD>
</TR>

</TABLE>


<P>
<TABLE width="100%" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-size: 10pt">

<TR valign="top" style="font-size: 10pt; color: #000000; background: transparent">
    <TD width="1%" nowrap align="right">8.</TD>
    <TD width="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD>The Agent may from time to time, after consultation with the Borrower and
the Lenders, determine and notify to all Parties any amendments which are
required to be made to this Schedule in order to comply with any change in
law, regulation or any requirements from time to time imposed by the
European Central Bank (or, in any case, any other authority which replaces
all or any of its functions) and any such determination shall, in the
absence of manifest error, be conclusive and binding on all Parties.</TD>
</TR>


</TABLE>

<P align="center" style="font-size: 10pt">- 91 -
</DIV>
